performers for its upcoming professional interactive dinner theatre shows directed by Janice Luise-Lutkus. <span class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span class="text_exposed_show">Shows include interactive comedy wedding and murder mystery performances.<br /> <br />  On-going auditions will take place by appointment on Sunday’s. Actors should bring a headshot and resume and be prepared to read from the script. Serious artists only.<br /> <br /> Appointments are suggested and can be made by calling 860-309-1341.<br /> <br /> AspenDream Productions™, looks for a balanced mix of ages, and sizes, as well as performers whose strength is acting, singing, or dancing. <br /> <br /> Talent is only one of the attributes sought in company members: potential, a high degree of motivation, maturity, and commitment are other qualities that successful company members need to demonstrate. <br /> <br />  We do an exceptional job for our clients and only accept outstanding artists who are motivated with great attitudes.<br /> <br />  REQUIRMENTS:<br /> <br /> Comedic stereotypical characters. Currently seeking Female and Males of all shapes and sizes that work as a team. Must be 18.  Groom, Bride, Mobsters, Girlfriend, Mama, etc.<br /> <br />  AspenDream Productions™ requires all artists to have previous theatrical experience. Strong improv experience preferred. Transportation required. Must be willing to travel. Must reside in CT.  Stipend.<br /> <br />  WHEN ARE SHOWS:<br /> <br /> Shows generally held on various Friday and Saturday nights. Rehearsals held in Harwinton on Sundays. Shows throughout CT and Western MA. <br /> <br />  Send head shot and resumes after you have reviewed website to: Janice&#064;AspenDreamProductions.com. interactive comedy wedding and murder mystery performances.<br /> <br />  On-going auditions will take place by appointment on Sunday’s. Actors should bring a headshot and resume and be prepared to read from the script. Serious artists only.<br /> <br /> Appointments are suggested and can be made by calling 860-309-1341.<br /> <br /> AspenDream Productions™, looks for a balanced mix of ages, and sizes, as well as performers whose strength is acting, singing, or dancing. <br /> <br /> Talent is only one of the attributes sought in company members: potential, a high degree of motivation, maturity, and commitment are other qualities that successful company members need to demonstrate. <br /> <br />  We do an exceptional job for our clients and only accept outstanding artists who are motivated with great attitudes.<br /> <br />  REQUIRMENTS:<br /> <br /> Comedic stereotypical characters. Currently seeking Female and Males of all shapes and sizes that work as a team. Must be 18.  Groom, Bride, Mobsters, Girlfriend, Mama, etc.<br /> <br />  AspenDream Productions™ requires all artists to have previous theatrical experience. Strong improv experience preferred. Transportation required. Must be willing to travel. Must reside in CT.  Stipend.<br /> <br />  WHEN ARE SHOWS:<br /> <br /> Shows generally held on various Friday and Saturday nights. Rehearsals held in Harwinton on Sundays. Shows throughout CT and Western MA. <br /> <br />  Send head shot and resumes after you have reviewed website to: Janice&#064;AspenDreamProductions.com.
